\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Base class for all Database\+Platforms. The Database\+Platforms are the central point of abstraction of platform-\/specific behaviors, features and SQL dialects. They are a passive source of information.

\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Todo}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{todo__todo000001}{Todo}}]Remove any unnecessary methods. \end{DoxyRefDesc}

\index{AbstractPlatform@{AbstractPlatform}!convertBooleans@{convertBooleans}}
\index{convertBooleans@{convertBooleans}!AbstractPlatform@{AbstractPlatform}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{convertBooleans()}{convertBooleans()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily convert\+Booleans (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$item }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Some platforms need the boolean values to be converted.

The default conversion in this implementation converts to integers (false =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 0, true =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 1).

Note\+: if the input is not a boolean the original input might be returned.

There are two contexts when converting booleans\+: Literals and Prepared Statements. This method should handle the literal case


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
mixed & {\em \$item} & A boolean or an array of them.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
mixed A boolean database value or an array of them. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily convert\+Booleans\+To\+Database\+Value (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$item }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

This method should handle the prepared statements case. When there is no distinction, it\textquotesingle{}s OK to use the same method.

Note\+: if the input is not a boolean the original input might be returned.

\index{AbstractPlatform@{AbstractPlatform}!getBetweenExpression@{getBetweenExpression}}
\index{getBetweenExpression@{getBetweenExpression}!AbstractPlatform@{AbstractPlatform}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{getBetweenExpression()}{getBetweenExpression()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily get\+Between\+Expression (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$expression,  }\item[{}]{\$value1,  }\item[{}]{\$value2 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the SQL that checks if an expression evaluates to a value between two values.

The parameter \$expression is checked if it is between \$value1 and \$value2.

Note\+: There is a slight difference in the way BETWEEN works on some databases. \href{http://www.w3schools.com/sql/sql_between.asp}{\texttt{ http\+://www.\+w3schools.\+com/sql/sql\+\_\+between.\+asp}}. If you want complete database independence you should avoid using between().

\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{deprecated__deprecated000094}{Deprecated}}]Use BETWEEN in SQL instead.\end{DoxyRefDesc}



\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
string & {\em \$expression} & The value to compare to. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$value1} & The lower value to compare with. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$value2} & The higher value to compare with.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
string The logical expression. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily get\+Column\+Declaration\+List\+SQL (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{array}]{\$columns }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Gets declaration of a number of columns in bulk.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
mixed\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]}\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]} & {\em \$columns} & A multidimensional associative array. The first dimension determines the column name, while the second dimension is keyed with the name of the properties of the column being declared as array indexes. Currently, the types of supported column properties are as follows\+:\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
length Integer value that determines the maximum length of the text column. If this argument is missing the column should be declared to have the longest length allowed by the DBMS.

default Text value to be used as default for this column.

notnull Boolean flag that indicates whether this column is constrained to not be set to null. charset Text value with the default CHARACTER SET for this column. collation Text value with the default COLLATION for this column. unique unique constraint

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
string 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Obtains DBMS specific SQL code portion needed to declare a generic type column to be used in statements like CREATE TABLE.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
string & {\em \$name} & The name the column to be declared. \\
\hline
mixed\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]} & {\em \$column} & An associative array with the name of the properties of the column being declared as array indexes. Currently, the types of supported column properties are as follows\+:\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
length Integer value that determines the maximum length of the text column. If this argument is missing the column should be declared to have the longest length allowed by the DBMS.

default Text value to be used as default for this column.

notnull Boolean flag that indicates whether this column is constrained to not be set to null. charset Text value with the default CHARACTER SET for this column. collation Text value with the default COLLATION for this column. unique unique constraint check column check constraint column\+Definition a string that defines the complete column

string DBMS specific SQL code portion that should be used to declare the column.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily get\+Count\+Expression (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$column }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the SQL snippet to get the number of rows (without a NULL value) of a column.

If a \textquotesingle{}$\ast$\textquotesingle{} is used instead of a column the number of selected rows is returned.

\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{deprecated__deprecated000079}{Deprecated}}]Use COUNT() in SQL instead.\end{DoxyRefDesc}

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
string Generated SQL including a COUNT aggregate function. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily get\+List\+Table\+Indexes\+SQL (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$table,  }\item[{}]{\$database = {\ttfamily null} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the list of indexes for the current database.

The current database parameter is optional but will always be passed when using the Schema\+Manager API and is the database the given table is in.

Attention\+: Some platforms only support current\+Database when they are connected with that database. Cross-\/database information schema requests may be impossible.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_doctrine_1_1_d_b_a_l_1_1_platforms_1_1_abstract_platform_a821885993ed4c14395fb2d899522c956}\label{class_doctrine_1_1_d_b_a_l_1_1_platforms_1_1_abstract_platform_a821885993ed4c14395fb2d899522c956}} 
\index{AbstractPlatform@{AbstractPlatform}!getReadLockSQL@{getReadLockSQL}}
\index{getReadLockSQL@{getReadLockSQL}!AbstractPlatform@{AbstractPlatform}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{getReadLockSQL()}{getReadLockSQL()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily get\+Read\+Lock\+SQL (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the SQL snippet to append to any SELECT statement which locks rows in shared read lock.

This defaults to the ANSI SQL \char`\"{}\+FOR UPDATE\char`\"{}, which is an exclusive lock (Write). Some database vendors allow to lighten this constraint up to be a real read lock.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
string 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{AbstractPlatform@{AbstractPlatform}!getTemporaryTableSQL@{getTemporaryTableSQL}}
\index{getTemporaryTableSQL@{getTemporaryTableSQL}!AbstractPlatform@{AbstractPlatform}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{getTemporaryTableSQL()}{getTemporaryTableSQL()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily get\+Temporary\+Table\+SQL (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the required SQL string that fits between CREATE ... TABLE to create the table as a temporary table.

Should be overridden in driver classes to return the correct string for the specific database type.

The default is to return the string \char`\"{}\+TEMPORARY\char`\"{} -\/ this will result in a SQL error for any database that does not support temporary tables, or that requires a different SQL command from \char`\"{}\+CREATE TEMPORARY TABLE\char`\"{}.

\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{deprecated__deprecated000100}{Deprecated}}]\end{DoxyRefDesc}


\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
string The string required to be placed between \char`\"{}\+CREATE\char`\"{} and \char`\"{}\+TABLE\char`\"{} to generate a temporary table, if possible. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_doctrine_1_1_d_b_a_l_1_1_platforms_1_1_abstract_platform_ad88238abfcf236ac74537ad04df56493}\label{class_doctrine_1_1_d_b_a_l_1_1_platforms_1_1_abstract_platform_ad88238abfcf236ac74537ad04df56493}}

\index{AbstractPlatform@{AbstractPlatform}!quoteIdentifier@{quoteIdentifier}}
\index{quoteIdentifier@{quoteIdentifier}!AbstractPlatform@{AbstractPlatform}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{quoteIdentifier()}{quoteIdentifier()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily quote\+Identifier (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$str }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Quotes a string so that it can be safely used as a table or column name, even if it is a reserved word of the platform. This also detects identifier chains separated by dot and quotes them independently.

NOTE\+: Just because you CAN use quoted identifiers doesn\textquotesingle{}t mean you SHOULD use them. In general, they end up causing way more problems than they solve.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
string & {\em \$str} & The identifier name to be quoted.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
string The quoted identifier string. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
